Hello,

   Thanks for (re)trying. As far as I can tell from your screenshot  - you
have to install bundler first - sorry for the confusion it's not a "home
grown" script (e.g. bundle.rb)  it is ruby's package tool.
    Use
     $ gem install bundler         # that gives you the bundle command

    Learn more about bundler @ https://bundler.io
   Cheers. Prost.
